name:A‚Äçn‚Äço‚Äçn‚Äçy‚Äçm‚Äço‚Äçu‚Äçs‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

rating:4
posted:Posted November 4, 2023
msg:1. External environment: 8 points: The hotel is composed of several low-rise buildings. Entering the hotel is a short winding mountain road. It gives you a quiet resort feel. There is an outdoor viewing platform and swings on the lawn between the buildings. Like the Moon Lift Chair, the overall external environment and layout are quite ok. The only drawback is that the lake area facing the hotel is a small bay and there is no open lake view. However, in contrast, the hotel is located very far from the southeast lake area pier. It's close, just a few minutes' taxi ride away.
2. Internal environment: 7 points: The interior of the building is decorated in a modern style. The white gauze curtains in the corridor and the brown door of the room match well. I booked a view room and communicated with Xiao Zheng at the front desk to help me upgrade to a lake view room. The interior decoration of the room is simple and quite satisfactory. , I personally feel that compared to the color matching of the corridor and the texture of the door, the decoration aesthetics in the room are a bit boring and could be more refined. The three-separated design of the bathroom, washroom and shower is well received, especially the sink basin is deep and wide enough and is not easy to splash. The water and room hygiene are okay, the faucet is very bright, the towels, bath towels, sheets and quilts look relatively clean. If the balcony door in the room is not closed, there will be larger hard-shelled bugs running in. Please pay attention to check this.
3. Service 9 points: From booking to check-in, Xiao Zheng's service at the front desk was very good. When checking in, he upgraded the room type. He proactively asked about the disposable items and the usage time of the pots that came with the package. The communication was timely and he also gave them as a gift when checking out. The snacks and water were very considerate; the guest room was also cleaned in a timely manner. When I went to have breakfast in the morning, the room was tidied up when I came back. The man who drove the shuttle bus when we stayed in Building 2 was also very enthusiastic and took the initiative to inform us in the future. For the breakfast route, there are both Chinese and Western food for breakfast, with a relatively complete range and a passing grade or above.
4. Overall, it depends on how you want to go to Qiandao Lake, and then choose a suitable hotel based on your needs. This hotel is quite suitable to stay in the Southeast Lake District. It is also cost-effective to avoid peak travel!
